.lux-btn:hover::before{
  left:120%;
}

/* RIPPLE */
.lux-btn span.ripple{
  position:absolute;
  border-radius:50%;
  transform:scale(0);
  animation:ripple .6s linear;
  background:rgba(255,255,255,.6);
}
@keyframes ripple{
  to{
    transform:scale(4);
    opacity:0;
  }
}

/* MOBILE */
@media(max-width:480px){
  .lux-auth-panel{
    flex-direction:column;
  }
  .lux-btn{
    width:100%;
    justify-content:center;
  }
}
</style>
<script>
document.querySelectorAll('.lux-btn').forEach(btn=>{
  btn.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    const circle = document.createElement('span');
    const diameter = Math.max(this.clientWidth, this.clientHeight);
    const radius = diameter / 2;

    circle.style.width = circle.style.height = `${diameter}px`;
    circle.style.left = `${e.clientX - this.getBoundingClientRect().left - radius}px`;
    circle.style.top  = `${e.clientY - this.getBoundingClientRect().top - radius}px`;
    circle.classList.add('ripple');

    const ripple = this.querySelector('.ripple');
    if(ripple) ripple.remove();

    this.appendChild(circle);
  });
});
</script>

            <script>
              window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                const passwordInputTrigger = document.querySelector('#password_input_trigger');
                const passwordInput = document.querySelector('#password_input');
                passwordInputTrigger.onclick = () => {
                  if (passwordInput.type === 'password') {
                    passwordInput.type = 'text';
                    return;
                  }
                  passwordInput.type = 'password';
                };
              });
            </script>
          </div>

<style>

.lux-announce-vertical{
  height:70px;                 /* tinggi 1 berita */
  overflow:hidden;
  background:linear-gradient(180deg,#000,#111);
  border:1px solid rgba(255,215,0,.35);
  border-radius:14px;
  padding:0 14px;
  display:flex;
  align-items:center;
  font-family:Segoe UI,sans-serif;
}

.lux-announce-track{
  list-style:none;
  margin:0;
  padding:0;
  transition:transform .7s ease-in-out;
}

.lux-announce-track li{
  height:70px;
  display:flex;
  align-items:center;
  color:#ffd700;
  line-height:1.4;
}
</style>

<script>
const track = document.getElementById("luxAnnounceTrack");
const items = track.children;
const itemHeight = 70;
let index = 0;
let interval;

function slideUp(){
  index++;
  track.style.transform = `translateY(-${index * itemHeight}px)`;

  if(index === items.length){
    setTimeout(()=>{
      track.style.transition = "none";
      track.style.transform = "translateY(0)";
      index = 0;
      setTimeout(()=>track.style.transition = "transform .7s ease-in-out",50);
    },700);
  }
}

function start(){
  interval = setInterval(slideUp, 4000);
}
function stop(){
  clearInterval(interval);
}

start();
track.parentElement.addEventListener("mouseenter",stop);
track.parentElement.addEventListener("mouseleave",start);
</script>

<script>
let lastScroll = 0;
const dock = document.querySelector('.aurumDock');

window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
  const currentScroll = window.pageYOffset;

  if (currentScroll > lastScroll && currentScroll > 120) {
    dock.classList.add('is-visible');
  } else {
    dock.classList.remove('is-visible');
  }

  lastScroll = currentScroll;
});
</script>
